 </mrow>\n                <mo>.</mo>\n              </mtd>\n            </mtr>\n          </mtable>\n        </mrow>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}x&amp;\\equiv 0{\\pmod {3}}\\\\x&amp;\\equiv 3{\\pmod {4}}\\\\x&amp;\\equiv 4{\\pmod {5}}.\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/05184a57666ddba2a8941b6f2e575b6ab1f30e9a\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -4.005ex; width:17.835ex; height:9.176ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}x&amp;\\equiv 0{\\pmod {3}}\\\\x&amp;\\equiv 3{\\pmod {4}}\\\\x&amp;\\equiv 4{\\pmod {5}}.\\end{aligned}}}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Systematic_search\">Systematic search</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11\" title=\"Edit section: Systematic search\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>It is easy to check whether a value of <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">x</span> is a solution: it suffices to compute the remainder of the <a href=\"/wiki/Euclidean_division\" title=\"Euclidean division\">Euclidean division</a> of <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">x</span> by each <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>n</i><sub><i>i</i></sub></span>. Thus, to find the solution, it suffices to check successively the integers from <span class=\"texhtml\">0</span> to <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">N</span> until finding the solution.\n</p><p>Although very simple this method is very inefficient: for the simple example considered here, <span class=\"texhtml\">40</span> integers (including <span class=\"texhtml\">0</span>) have to be checked for finding the solution, which is <span class=\"texhtml\">39</span>. This is an <a href=\"/wiki/Exponential_time\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Exponential time\">exponential time</a> algorithm, as the size of the input is, up to a constant factor, the number of digits of <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">N</span>, and the average number of operations is of the order of <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">N</span>.\n</p><p>Therefore, this method is rarely used, neither for hand-written computation nor on computers.\n</p>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Search_by_sieving\">Search by sieving</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12\" title=\"Edit section: Search by sieving\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The search of the solution may be made dramatically faster by sieving. For this method, we suppose, without loss of generality, that <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle 0\\leq a_{i}&lt;n_{i}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mn>0</mn>\n        <mo>&#x2264;<!-- \u2264 --></mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>a</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&lt;</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle 0\\leq a_{i}&lt;n_{i}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2f3a3d38b47b2a147cd76af43160deee6140a731\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:11.583ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle 0\\leq a_{i}&lt;n_{i}}\"/></span> (if it were not the case, it would suffice to replace each <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle a_{i}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>a</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle a_{i}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0bc77764b2e74e64a63341054fa90f3e07db275f\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.029ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"a_{i}\"/></span> by the remainder of its division by <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{i}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle n_{i}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/57f87f905ba5a4d8c691ccaecd65fc47bd007ba4\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.194ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"n_{i}\"/></span>). This implies that the solution belongs to the <a href=\"/wiki/Arithmetic_progression\" title=\"Arithmetic progression\">arithmetic progression</a>\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle a_{1},a_{1}+n_{1},a_{1}+2n_{1},\\ldots }\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>a</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>a</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>a</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mn>2</mn>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2026;<!-- \u2026 --></mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle a_{1},a_{1}+n_{1},a_{1}+2n_{1},\\ldots }</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/590744fba5423bad6e1ae8a075908f9790d04926\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:24.418ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle a_{1},a_{1}+n_{1},a_{1}+2n_{1},\\ldots }\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>By testing the values of these numbers modulo <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{2},}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle n_{2},}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/01fc2a1d78988b45a78b11bf2dea0876cb16a628\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.096ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle n_{2},}\"/></span> one eventually finds a solution <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle x_{2}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>x</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle x_{2}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d7af1b928f06e4c7e3e8ebfd60704656719bd766\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.384ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"x_{2}\"/></span> of the two first congruences. Then the solution belongs to the arithmetic progression \n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle x_{2},x_{2}+n_{1}n_{2},x_{2}+2n_{1}n_{2},\\ldots }\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>x</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>x</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>x</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mn>2</mn>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2026;<!-- \u2026 --></mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle x_{2},x_{2}+n_{1}n_{2},x_{2}+2n_{1}n_{2},\\ldots }</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5188b0f0af1dd87f10761a118ecf582067c9df1c\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:29.616ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle x_{2},x_{2}+n_{1}n_{2},x_{2}+2n_{1}n_{2},\\ldots }\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Testing the values of these numbers modulo <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{3},}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>3</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle n_{3},}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/14d1e92ae65bb5b20bf475a15b4c8df5d71c58d9\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.096ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle n_{3},}\"/></span>, and continuing until every modulus has been tested gives eventually the solution.\n</p><p>This method is faster if the moduli have been ordered by decreasing value, that is if <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{1}&gt;n_{2}&gt;\\cdots &gt;n_{k}.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&gt;</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&gt;</mo>\n        <mo>&#x22EF;<!-- \u22ef --></mo>\n        <mo>&gt;</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>k</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle n_{1}&gt;n_{2}&gt;\\cdots &gt;n_{k}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ba4dd6fff3697e044c65ec36913cc6ceb4715d53\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:20.047ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle n_{1}&gt;n_{2}&gt;\\cdots &gt;n_{k}.}\"/></span> For the example, this gives the following computation. We consider first the numbers that are congruent to 4 modulo 5 (the largest modulus), which are 4, <span class=\"nowrap\">9 = 4 + 5</span>, <span class=\"nowrap\">14 = 9 + 5</span>, ... For each of them, compute the remainder by 4 (the second largest modulus) until getting a number congruent to 3 modulo 4. Then one can proceed  by adding <span class=\"nowrap\">20 = 5\u00d74</span> at each step, and computing only the remainders by 3. This gives\n</p>\n<dl><dd>4 mod 4 \u2192 0. Continue</dd>\n<dd>4 + 5 = 9 mod 4 \u21921.  Continue</dd>\n<dd>9 + 5 = 14 mod 4 \u2192 2. Continue</dd>\n<dd>14 + 5 = 19 mod 4 \u2192 3. OK, continue by considering remainders modulo 3 and adding 5\u00d74 = 20 each time</dd>\n<dd>19 mod 3 \u2192 1. Continue</dd>\n<dd>19 + 20 = 39 mod 3 \u2192 0. OK, this is the result.</dd></dl>\n<p>This method works well for hand-written computation with a product of moduli that is not too big. However, it is much slower than other methods, for very large products of moduli. Although dramatically faster than the systematic search, this method also has an <a href=\"/wiki/Exponential_time\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Exponential time\">exponential time</a> complexity and is therefore not used on computers.\n</p>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Using_the_existence_construction\">Using the existence construction</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13\" title=\"Edit section: Using the existence construction\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The <a href=\"#Existence_(constructive_proof)\">constructive existence proof</a> shows that, in the <a href=\"#Case_of_two_moduli\">case of two moduli</a>, the solution may be obtained by the computation of the <a href=\"/wiki/B%C3%A9zout_coefficients\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"B\u00e9zout coefficients\">B\u00e9zout coefficients</a> of the moduli, followed by a few multiplications, additions and reductions modulo <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{1}n_{2}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle n_{1}n_{2}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a70ec72e416c0e2120ab2480be2bf67cc40817bd\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:4.898ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"n_{1}n_{2}\"/></span> (for getting a result in the interval <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle (0,n_{1}n_{2}-1)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mn>0</mn>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <mn>1</mn>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle (0,n_{1}n_{2}-1)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0bb6d7d2f68a665f269dc20e09820ed709e54276\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:12.906ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle (0,n_{1}n_{2}-1)}\"/></span>). As the B\u00e9zout's coefficients may be computed with the <a href=\"/wiki/Extended_Euclidean_algorithm\" title=\"Extended Euclidean algorithm\">extended Euclidean algorithm</a>, the whole computation, at most, has a quadratic <a href=\"/wiki/Time_complexity\" title=\"Time complexity\">time complexity</a> of <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle O((s_{1}+s_{2})^{2}),}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>O</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>s</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>s</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msup>\n          <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle O((s_{1}+s_{2})^{2}),}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f95593c98bb17539448c320c3952a415739842e5\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:14.223ex; height:3.176ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle O((s_{1}+s_{2})^{2}),}\"/></span> where <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle s_{i}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>s</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle s_{i}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cfda82668232cbdc0874ed28ab8b6079420d1ffe\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.89ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"s_{i}\"/></span> denotes the number of digits of <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{i}.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle n_{i}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81ebb140df365bcc7a5b990ca37dfb37bd723d47\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.841ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle n_{i}.}\"/></span>\n</p><p>For more than two moduli, the method for two moduli allows the replacement of any two congruences by a single congruence modulo the product of the moduli. Iterating this process provides eventually the solution with a complexity, which is quadratic in the number of digits of the product of all moduli. This quadratic time complexity does not depend on the order in which the moduli are regrouped. One may regroup the two first moduli, then regroup the resulting modulus with the next one, and so on. This strategy is the easiest to implement, but it also requires more computation involving large numbers.\n</p><p>Another strategy consists in partitioning the moduli in pairs whose product have comparable sizes (as much as possible), applying, in parallel, the method of two moduli to each pair, and iterating with a number of moduli approximatively divided by two. This method allows an easy parallelization of the algorithm. Also, if fast algorithms (that is algorithms working in <a href=\"/wiki/Quasilinear_time\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Quasilinear time\">quasilinear time</a>) are used for the basic operations, this method provides an algorithm for the whole computation that works in quasilinear time.\n</p><p>On the current example (which has only three moduli), both strategies are identical and work as follows.\n</p><p><a href=\"/wiki/B%C3%A9zout%27s_identity\" title=\"B\u00e9zout&#39;s identity\">B\u00e9zout's identity</a> for 3 and 4 is\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle 1\\times 4+(-1)\\times 3=1.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mn>1</mn>\n        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- \u00d7 --></mo>\n        <mn>4</mn>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <mn>1</mn>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- \u00d7 --></mo>\n        <mn>3</mn>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>1.</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle 1\\times 4+(-1)\\times 3=1.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/82cf791385f6a770fd9ead37152a54d45a40867c\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:21.696ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle 1\\times 4+(-1)\\times 3=1.}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Putting this in the formula given for proving the existence gives \n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle 4\\times 0+(-3)\\times 3=-9}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mn>4</mn>\n        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- \u00d7 --></mo>\n        <mn>0</mn>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <mn>3</mn>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- \u00d7 --></mo>\n        <mn>3</mn>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <mn>9</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle 4\\times 0+(-3)\\times 3=-9}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5aef1795152cec9e53141901249d972e1ec4fe9d\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:22.858ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle 4\\times 0+(-3)\\times 3=-9}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>for a solution of the two first congruences, the other solutions being obtained by adding to \u22129 any multiple of <span class=\"nowrap\">3\u00d74 = 12</span>. One may continue with any of these solutions, but the solution <span class=\"nowrap\">3 = \u22129 +12</span> is smaller (in absolute value) and thus leads probably to an easier computation\n</p><p>B\u00e9zout identity for 5 and 3\u00d74 = 12 is\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle 5\\times 5+(-2)\\times 12=1.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mn>5</mn>\n        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- \u00d7 --></mo>\n        <mn>5</mn>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <mn>2</mn>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- \u00d7 --></mo>\n        <mn>12</mn>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>1.</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle 5\\times 5+(-2)\\times 12=1.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3af78d5c8b3372cc55c427fab588145a3a791a8d\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:22.859ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle 5\\times 5+(-2)\\times 12=1.}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Applying the same formula again, we get a solution of the problem:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle 25\\times 3-24\\times 4=-21.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mn>25</mn>\n        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- \u00d7 --></mo>\n        <mn>3</mn>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <mn>24</mn>\n        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- \u00d7 --></mo>\n        <mn>4</mn>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <mn>21.</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle 25\\times 3-24\\times 4=-21.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2462c0245799cd44cf4b3262d1fde9cfdd5d3a2c\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:23.374ex; height:2.343ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle 25\\times 3-24\\times 4=-21.}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>The other solutions are obtained by adding any multiple of <span class=\"nowrap\">3\u00d74\u00d75 = 60</span>, and the smallest positive solution is <span class=\"nowrap\">\u221221 + 60 = 39</span>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"As_a_linear_Diophantine_system\">As a linear Diophantine system</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14\" title=\"Edit section: As a linear Diophantine system\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The system of congruences solved by the Chinese remainder theorem may be rewritten as a <a href=\"/wiki/Diophantine_equation#System_of_linear_Diophantine_equations\" title=\"Diophantine equation\">system of simultaneous linear Diophantine equations</a>:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}x&amp;=a_{1}+x_{1}n_{1}\\\\&amp;\\vdots \\\\x&amp;=a_{k}+x_{k}n_{k},\\end{aligned}}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n          <mtable columnalign=\"right left right left right left right left right left right left\" rowspacing=\"3pt\" columnspacing=\"0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em\" displaystyle=\"true\">\n            <mtr>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi>x</mi>\n              </mtd>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi></mi>\n                <mo>=</mo>\n                <msub>\n                  <mi>a</mi>\n                  <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                    <mn>1</mn>\n                  </mrow>\n                </msub>\n                <mo>+</mo>\n                <msub>\n                  <mi>x</mi>\n                  <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                    <mn>1</mn>\n                  </mrow>\n                </msub>\n                <msub>\n                  <mi>n</mi>\n                  <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                    <mn>1</mn>\n                  </mrow>\n                </msub>\n              </mtd>\n            </mtr>\n            <mtr>\n              <mtd />\n              <mtd>\n                <mi></mi>\n                <mo>&#x22EE;<!-- \u22ee --></mo>\n              </mtd>\n            </mtr>\n            <mtr>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi>x</mi>\n              </mtd>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi></mi>\n                <mo>=</mo>\n                <msub>\n                  <mi>a</mi>\n                  <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                    <mi>k</mi>\n                  </mrow>\n                </msub>\n                <mo>+</mo>\n                <msub>\n                  <mi>x</mi>\n                  <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                    <mi>k</mi>\n                  </mrow>\n                </msub>\n                <msub>\n                  <mi>n</mi>\n                  <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                    <mi>k</mi>\n                  </mrow>\n                </msub>\n                <mo>,</mo>\n              </mtd>\n            </mtr>\n          </mtable>\n        </mrow>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}x&amp;=a_{1}+x_{1}n_{1}\\\\&amp;\\vdots \\\\x&amp;=a_{k}+x_{k}n_{k},\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7716745a5ed43fb42b34c22fa98aecd211e69738\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -4.505ex; width:15.887ex; height:10.176ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}x&amp;=a_{1}+x_{1}n_{1}\\\\&amp;\\vdots \\\\x&amp;=a_{k}+x_{k}n_{k},\\end{aligned}}}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>where the unknown integers are <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle x}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>x</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle x}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;\" alt=\"x\"/></span> and the <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle x_{i}.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>x</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle x_{i}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ca686849ad350b47ebab4a394b66d84d5fa942bf\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.776ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"x_{i}.\"/></span> Therefore, every general method for solving such systems may be used for finding the solution of Chinese remainder theorem, such as the reduction of the matrix of the system to <a href=\"/wiki/Smith_normal_form\" title=\"Smith normal form\">Smith normal form</a> or <a href=\"/wiki/Hermite_normal_form\" title=\"Hermite normal form\">Hermite normal form</a>. However, as usual when using a general algorithm for a more specific problem, this approach is less efficient than the method of the preceding section, based on a direct use of <a href=\"/wiki/B%C3%A9zout%27s_identity\" title=\"B\u00e9zout&#39;s identity\">B\u00e9zout's identity</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Over_principal_ideal_domains\">Over principal ideal domains</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15\" title=\"Edit section: Over principal ideal domains\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>In <a href=\"#Theorem_statement\">\u00a7&#160;Theorem statement</a>, the Chinese remainder theorem has been stated in three different ways: in terms of remainders, of congruences, and of a ring isomorphism. The statement in terms of remainders does not apply, in general, to <a href=\"/wiki/Principal_ideal_domain\" title=\"Principal ideal domain\">principal ideal domains</a>, as remainders are not defined in such rings. However, the two other versions make sense over a principal ideal domain <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>R</i></span>: it suffices to replace \"integer\" by \"element of the domain\" and <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\mathbb {Z} }\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n          <mi mathvariant=\"double-struck\">Z</mi>\n        </mrow>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\mathbb {Z} }</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/449494a083e0a1fda2b61c62b2f09b6bee4633dc\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.55ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"\\mathbb {Z} \"/></span> by  <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>R</i></span>. These two versions of the theorem are true in this context, because the proofs (except for the first existence proof), are based on <a href=\"/wiki/Euclid%27s_lemma\" title=\"Euclid&#39;s lemma\">Euclid's lemma</a> and <a href=\"/wiki/B%C3%A9zout%27s_identity\" title=\"B\u00e9zout&#39;s identity\">B\u00e9zout's identity</a>, which are true over every principal domain.\n</p><p>However, in general, the theorem is only an existence theorem and does not provide any way for computing the solution, unless one has an algorithm for computing the coefficients of B\u00e9zout's identity.\n</p>\n<h2><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Over_univariate_polynomial_rings_and_Euclidean_domains\">Over univariate polynomial rings and Euclidean domains</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16\" title=\"Edit section: Over univariate polynomial rings and Euclidean domains\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The statement in terms of remainders given in <a href=\"#Theorem_statement\">\u00a7&#160;Theorem statement</a> cannot be generalized to any principal ideal domain, but its generalization to <a href=\"/wiki/Euclidean_domain\" title=\"Euclidean domain\">Euclidean domains</a> is straightforward. The <a href=\"/wiki/Univariate_polynomial\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Univariate polynomial\">univariate polynomials</a> over a <a href=\"/wiki/Field_(mathematics)\" title=\"Field (mathematics)\">field</a> is the typical example of a Euclidean domain, which is not the integers. Therefore, we state the theorem for the case of a ring of univariate domain <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle R=K[X]}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>R</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>K</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">[</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">]</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle R=K[X]}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b3fe87f64d3fb94108c78a00de91e770e01ea465\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:10.202ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle R=K[X]}\"/></span> over a field <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle K.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>K</mi>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle K.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1bb0e178e42abf16ef4e4c0b0f22aa235ad6e6e5\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.713ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"K.\"/></span> For getting the theorem for a general Euclidean domain, it suffices to replace the degree by the <a href=\"/wiki/Euclidean_function\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Euclidean function\">Euclidean function</a> of the Euclidean domain.\n</p><p>The Chinese remainder theorem for polynomials is thus: Let <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>P</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3fb38d4b78c121420a4c0ea74ee28ec57d4a6cee\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.081ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}\"/></span> (the moduli) be,  for <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>i</i>=1, ..., <i>k</i></span>, <a href=\"/wiki/Pairwise_coprime\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Pairwise coprime\">pairwise coprime</a> polynomials in <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle R=K[X]}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>R</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>K</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">[</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">]</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle R=K[X]}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b3fe87f64d3fb94108c78a00de91e770e01ea465\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:10.202ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle R=K[X]}\"/></span>. Let <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle d_{i}=\\deg P_{i}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>d</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>deg</mi>\n        <mo>&#x2061;<!-- \u2061 --></mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>P</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle d_{i}=\\deg P_{i}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/279ad2d31dd06e5eb23d10a113ea378f36ad924b\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:6.081ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}\"/></span>, and <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle D}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>D</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle D}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f34a0c600395e5d4345287e21fb26efd386990e6\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.655ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle d_{i}.}\"/></span>\nIf <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle A_{i}(X),\\ldots ,A_{k}(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>A</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2026;<!-- \u2026 --></mo>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>A</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>k</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle A_{i}(X),\\ldots ,A_{k}(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8ca5c466fd33910cb226735450bf3444a0b0c4a9\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:10.593ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle A_{i}(X)=0}\"/></span> or <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\deg A_{i}&lt;d_{i}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>deg</mi>\n        <mo>&#x2061;<!-- \u2061 --></mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>A</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&lt;</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>d</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\deg A_{i}&lt;d_{i}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/88e24fe31417c6fe3035226107c36d10bffcbca8\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:11.524ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle \\deg A_{i}&lt;d_{i}}\"/></span> for every <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>i</i></span>, then, there is one and only one polynomial <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>P</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf94167ebc67db1573e6be9e261cd0518e49e160\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.535ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"P(X)\"/></span>, such that <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\deg P&lt;D}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>deg</mi>\n        <mo>&#x2061;<!-- \u2061 --></mo>\n        <mi>P</mi>\n        <mo>&lt;</mo>\n        <mi>D</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\deg P&lt;D}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f13c34fe6dc4b8f0bd1347d998287b6af82ee7f4\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:10.643ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle \\deg P&lt;D}\"/></span> and the remainder of the <a href=\"/wiki/Euclidean_division\" title=\"Euclidean division\">Euclidean division</a> of <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>P</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf94167ebc67db1573e6be9e261cd0518e49e160\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.535ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"P(X)\"/></span> by <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>P</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3fb38d4b78c121420a4c0ea74ee28ec57d4a6cee\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.081ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}\"/></span> is <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle A_{i}(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>A</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle A_{i}(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/65234f04d0c04a746e9a35f609f03de7af3a8a11\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; However, the latter construction may be simplified by using, as follows, <a href=\"/wiki/Partial_fraction_decomposition\" title=\"Partial fraction decomposition\">partial fraction decomposition</a> href=\"/wiki/Lagrange_interpolation\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Lagrange interpolation\">Lagrange interpolation</a>. For this, consider <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">k</span> <a href=\"/wiki/Monic_polynomial\" title=\"Monic polynomial\">monic polynomials</a> of degree one:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)=X-x_{i}.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>P</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>x</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)=X-x_{i}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e112903a49b7cb6e4bffbb0c264b5966cb92ca16\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; The remainder of the division by <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>P</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3fb38d4b78c121420a4c0ea74ee28ec57d4a6cee\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.081ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}\"/></span> of a polynomial <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>P</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf94167ebc67db1573e6be9e261cd0518e49e160\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:2.713ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"K.\"/></span> Both Lagrange interpolation and Chinese remainder theorem assert the existence of a unique polynomial <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P(X),}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>P</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P(X),}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d4cb09d6828a3e79dad4b330ce7a022c3851974c\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P(X)=\\sum _{i=1}^{k}A_{i}{\\frac {Q_{i}(X)}{Q_{i}(x_{i})}}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img width:22.978ex; height:7.343ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P(X)=\\sum _{i=1}^{k}A_{i}{\\frac {Q_{i}(X)}{Q_{i}(x_{i})}}.}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Hermite_interpolation\">Hermite interpolation</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18\" title=\"Edit section: Hermite interpolation\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href=\"/wiki/Hermite_interpolation\" title=\"Hermite interpolation\">Hermite interpolation</a> is an application of the Chinese remainder theorem for univariate polynomials, which may involve moduli of arbitrary degrees (Lagrange interpolation involves only moduli of degree one).\n</p><p>The problem consists of finding a polynomial of the least possible degree, such that the polynomial and its first derivatives take given values at some fixed points.\n</p><p>More precisely, let <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle x_{1},\\ldots ,x_{k}}\">\n  <semantics>\n       </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2026;<!-- \u2026 --></mo>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>x</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>k</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle x_{1},\\ldots ,x_{k}}</annotation>\n width:35.016ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P(X)\\equiv P_{i}(X){\\pmod {(X-x_{i})^{r_{i}}}}.}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Conversely, any polynomial <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>P</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf94167ebc67db1573e6be9e261cd0518e49e160\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.535ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P(X)}\"/></span> that satisfies these <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" width:1.211ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"k\"/></span> congruences, in particular verifies, for any <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle i=1,\\ldots ,k}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle <mi>k</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle i=1,\\ldots ,k}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f2dd4cb0548150c5ac4440b8a1e3b4f6218bdfd1\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:11.453ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle i=1,\\ldots ,k}\"/></span>\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\"  <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>P</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>P</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mi>o</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>x</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msup>\n          <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <msub>\n              <mi>r</mi>\n              <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                <mi>i</mi>\n              </mrow>\n            </msub>\n            <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P(X)=P_{i}(X)+o(X-x_{i})^{r_{i}-1}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d99c01a8d551032213b5f5792c9ad6e298120c96\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:31.141ex; height:3.176ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P(X)=P_{i}(X)+o(X-x_{i})^{r_{i}-1}}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>therefore <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>P</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3fb38d4b78c121420a4c0ea74ee28ec57d4a6cee\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.081ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P_{i}(X)}\"/></span> is its Taylor polynomial of order <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle r_{i}-1}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>r</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \u2212 --></mo>\n        <mn>1</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle r_{i}-1}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8c02d62d5652fe73974a4203dedfc17970d26192\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle x_{i}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>x</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle x_{i}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e87000dd6142b81d041896a30fe58f0c3acb2158\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.129ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"x_{i}\"/></span>, that is, <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P(X)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>P</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P(X)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf94167ebc67db1573e6be9e261cd0518e49e160\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.535ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"P(X)\"/></span> solves the initial Hermite interpolation problem.\nThe Chinese remainder theorem asserts that there exists exactly one polynomial of degree less than the sum of the <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle r_{i},}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>r</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle r_{i},}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d81f302d02f0ebf0e167b0d51b248f11ffa5de2f\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.495ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle r_{i},}\"/></span> which satisfies these <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle k}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>k</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle k}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3c9a2c7b599b37105512c5d570edc034056dd40\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.211ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"k\"/></span> congruences.\n</p><p>There are several ways for computing the solution <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle P(X).}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>P</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>X</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle P(X).}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/eb295085d8a178b84342fcf9af619c7d9d7dbdf0\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.182ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle P(X).}\"/></span> One may use the method described at the beginning of <a href=\"#Over_univariate_polynomial_rings_and_Euclidean_domains\">\u00a7&#160;Over univariate polynomial rings and Euclidean domains</a>. One may also use the constructions given in <a href=\"#Existence_(constructive_proof)\">\u00a7&#160;Existence (constructive proof)</a> or <a href=\"#Existence_(direct_proof)\">\u00a7&#160;Existence (direct proof)</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Generalization_to_non-coprime_moduli\">Generalization to non-coprime moduli</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19\" title=\"Edit section: Generalization to non-coprime moduli\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The Chinese remainder theorem can be generalized to non-coprime moduli. Let <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle m,n,a,b}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mi>n</mi>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mi>a</mi>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mi>b</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle m,n,a,b}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6cd51f626c33ed2c60bb0001fe84854ec30b9c62\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:8.764ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle m,n,a,b}\"/></span> be any integers, let <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle g=\\gcd(m,n)}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>g</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mo movablelimits=\"true\" form=\"prefix\">gcd</mo>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mi>n</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle g=\\gcd(m,n)}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7aded282847eeec80c37ef14c4f0f9a5b4847501\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:13.98ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle g=\\gcd(m,n)}\"/></span>, and consider the system of congruences:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\" displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n          <mtable columnalign=\"right left right left right left right left right left right left\" rowspacing=\"3pt\" columnspacing=\"0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em\" displaystyle=\"true\">\n            <mtr>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi>x</mi>\n              </mtd>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi></mi>\n                <mo>&#x2261;<!-- \u2261 --></mo>\n                <mi>a</mi>\n                <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                  <mspace stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n                </mrow>\n              </mtd>\n            </mtr>\n            <mtr>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi>x</mi>\n              </mtd>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi></mi>\n                <mo>&#x2261;<!-- \u2261 --></mo>\n                <mi>b</mi>\n                <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                  <mspace
