stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n                </mrow>\n                <mo>,</mo>\n              </mtd>\n            </mtr>\n          </mtable>\n        </mrow>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}x&amp;\\equiv a{\\pmod {m}}\\\\x&amp;\\equiv b{\\pmod {n}},\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c556c991ef3bd8ceae8c1b2d3dfbfb3c41324be6\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -2.505ex; width:18.134ex; height:6.176ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}x&amp;\\equiv a{\\pmod {m}}\\\\x&amp;\\equiv b{\\pmod {n}},\\end{aligned}}}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>If <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle a\\equiv b{\\pmod {g}}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>a</mi>\n        <mo>&#x2261;<!-- \u2261 --></mo>\n        <mi>b</mi>\n        <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n          <mspace width=\"1em\" />\n          <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n          <mi>mod</mi>\n          <mspace width=\"0.333em\" />\n          <mi>g</mi>\n          <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        </mrow>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle a\\equiv b{\\pmod {g}}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5725a7f8ffb17cd370ec025eb07e8d0feb556a76\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:16.126ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle a\\equiv b{\\pmod {g}}}\"/></span>, then this system of equations has a unique solution modulo <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\operatorname {lcm} (m,n)=mn/g}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>lcm</mi>\n        <mo>&#x2061;<!-- \u2061 --></mo>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mi>n</mi>\n        <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mi>n</mi>\n        <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n          <mo>/</mo>\n        </mrow>\n        <mi>g</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\operatorname {lcm} (m,n)=mn/g}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5ea28a4554d603d390684be7b6f9cd67a5ba980a\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:18.705ex; height:2.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle \\operatorname {lcm} (m,n)=mn/g}\"/></span>. Otherwise, it has no solutions.\n</p><p>If we use <a href=\"/wiki/B%C3%A9zout%27s_identity\" title=\"B\u00e9zout&#39;s identity\">B\u00e9zout's identity</a> to write <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle g=um+vn}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>g</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>u</mi>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mi>v</mi>\n        <mi>n</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle g=um+vn}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/69b8c072f680ec6e68256c8935952c76721f247e\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:12.947ex; height:2.343ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle g=um+vn}\"/></span>, then the solution is\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle x={\\frac {avn+bum}{g}}.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>x</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mrow>\n              <mi>a</mi>\n              <mi>v</mi>\n              <mi>n</mi>\n              <mo>+</mo>\n              <mi>b</mi>\n              <mi>u</mi>\n              <mi>m</mi>\n            </mrow>\n            <mi>g</mi>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle x={\\frac {avn+bum}{g}}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a08c1fd492020fc3bb798f06ca65f0ca695a0be\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:16.871ex; height:5.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle x={\\frac {avn+bum}{g}}.}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>This defines an integer, as <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">g</span> divides both <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">m</span> and <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">n</span>. Otherwise, the proof is very similar to that for coprime moduli.\n</p>\n<h2><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Generalization_to_arbitrary_rings\">Generalization to arbitrary rings</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20\" title=\"Edit section: Generalization to arbitrary rings\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The Chinese remainder theorem can be generalized to any <a href=\"/wiki/Ring_(mathematics)\" title=\"Ring (mathematics)\">ring</a>, by using <a href=\"/wiki/Coprime_integers#Coprimality_in_ring_ideals\" title=\"Coprime integers\">coprime ideals</a> (also called <a href=\"/wiki/Ideal_(ring_theory)#Types_of_ideals\" title=\"Ideal (ring theory)\">comaximal ideals</a>). Two ideals <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">I</span> and <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">J</span> are coprime if there are elements <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle i\\in I}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>i</mi>\n        <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n        <mi>I</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle i\\in I}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2d740fe587228ce31b71c9628e089d1a9b37c6be\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.815ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"i\\in I\"/></span> and <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle j\\in J}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>j</mi>\n        <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n        <mi>J</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle j\\in J}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6f6d6a463cc24fcc2d0ad452450c7a9d845409a7\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.027ex; width:5.297ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"j\\in J\"/></span> such that <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle i+j=1.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>i</mi>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mi>j</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>1.</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle i+j=1.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/414a8ee0e2297b3231f934cf384bcd0192007c2c\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:9.509ex; height:2.509ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle i+j=1.}\"/></span> This relation plays the role of <a href=\"/wiki/B%C3%A9zout%27s_identity\" title=\"B\u00e9zout&#39;s identity\">B\u00e9zout's identity</a> in the proofs related to this generalization, which, otherwise are very similar. The generalization may be stated as follows.<sup id=\"cite_ref-16\" class=\"reference\"><a href=\"#cite_note-16\">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Let <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>I</i><sub>1</sub>, ..., <i>I<sub>k</sub></i></span> be <a href=\"/wiki/Two-sided_ideal\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Two-sided ideal\">two-sided ideals</a> of a ring <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle R}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>R</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle R}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"R\"/></span> and let <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>I</i></span> be their intersection. If the ideals are pairwise coprime, we have the <a href=\"/wiki/Ring_homomorphism\" title=\"Ring homomorphism\">isomorphism</a>: \n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span {I}}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5df1179993680ef18ba9de8746f572831663c7f1\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6d88084f0ce6b21a819684057ef0e480b900c0bc\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.819ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"{\\displaystyle I.}\"/></span>\nMoreover, if <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle R}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>R</mi>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle R}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;\" alt=\"R\"/></span> is <a href=\"/wiki/Commutative_ring\" title=\"Commutative ring\">commutative</a>, then the ideal intersection of pairwise coprime ideals is equal to their <a href=\"/wiki/Product_of_ideals\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Product of ideals\">product</a>; that is\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle I=I_{1}\\cap I_{2}\\cap \\cdots \\cap I_{k}=I_{1}I_{2}\\cdots I_{k},}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mi>I</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>I</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&#x2229;<!-- \u2229 --></mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>I</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&#x2229;<!-- \u2229          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>I</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>I</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&#x22EF;<!-- \u22ef --></mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>I</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>k</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle I=I_{1}\\cap I_{2}\\cap \\cdots \\cap I_{k}=I_{1}I_{2}\\cdots I_{k},}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img style=\"font-style:italic;\">I<sub>i</sub></span>  and <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">I<sub>j</sub></span> are coprime for <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>i</i> \u2260 <i>j</i></span>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Applications\">Applications</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21\" title=\"Edit section: Applications\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Sequence_numbering\">Sequence numbering</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22\" title=\"Edit section: Sequence numbering\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The Chinese remainder theorem has been used to construct a <a href=\"/wiki/G%C3%B6del_numbering_for_sequences\" title=\"G\u00f6del numbering for sequences\">G\u00f6del numbering for sequences</a>, which is involved in the proof of <a href=\"/wiki/G%C3%B6del%27s_incompleteness_theorems\" title=\"G\u00f6del&#39;s incompleteness theorems\">G\u00f6del's incompleteness theorems</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Fast_Fourier_transform\">Fast Fourier transform</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23\" title=\"Edit section: Fast Fourier transform\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The <a href=\"/wiki/Prime-factor_FFT_algorithm\" title=\"Prime-factor FFT algorithm\">prime-factor FFT algorithm</a> (also called Good-Thomas algorithm) uses the Chinese remainder theorem for reducing the computation of a <a href=\"/wiki/Fast_Fourier_transform\" title=\"Fast Fourier transform\">fast Fourier transform</a> of size <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{1}n_{2}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle n_{1}n_{2}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a70ec72e416c0e2120ab2480be2bf67cc40817bd\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:4.898ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"n_{1}n_{2}\"/></span> to the computation of two fast Fourier transforms of smaller sizes <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{1}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle n_{1}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ee784b70e772f55ede5e6e0bdc929994bff63413\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.449ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"n_{1}\"/></span> and <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{2}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>n</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/840e456e3058bc0be28e5cf653b170cdbfcc3be4\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.449ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"n_{2}\"/></span> (providing that <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{1}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n width:2.449ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"n_{1}\"/></span> and <span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle n_{2}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle n_{2}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/840e456e3058bc0be28e5cf653b170cdbfcc3be4\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.449ex; height:2.009ex;\" alt=\"n_{2}\"/></span> are coprime).\n</p>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Encryption\">Encryption</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24\" title=\"Edit section: Encryption\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Most <a href=\"/wiki/RSA_(cryptosystem)#Using_the_Chinese_remainder_algorithm\" title=\"RSA (cryptosystem)\">implementations of RSA use the Chinese remainder theorem</a> during signing of <a href=\"/wiki/HTTPS\" title=\"HTTPS\">HTTPS</a> certificates and during decryption.\n</p><p>The Chinese remainder theorem can also be used in <a href=\"/wiki/Secret_sharing\" title=\"Secret sharing\">secret sharing</a>, which consists of distributing a set of shares among a group of people who, all together (but no one alone), can recover a certain secret from the given set of shares. Each of the shares is represented in a congruence, and the solution of the system of congruences using the Chinese remainder theorem is the secret to be recovered. <a href=\"/wiki/Secret_sharing_using_the_Chinese_remainder_theorem\" title=\"Secret sharing using the Chinese remainder theorem\">Secret sharing using the Chinese remainder theorem</a> uses, along with the Chinese remainder theorem, special sequences of integers that guarantee the impossibility of recovering the secret from a set of shares with less than a certain <a href=\"/wiki/Cardinality\" title=\"Cardinality\">cardinality</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Range_ambiguity_resolution\">Range ambiguity resolution</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25\" title=\"Edit section: Range ambiguity resolution\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role=\"note\" class=\"hatnote navigation-not-searchable\">Main article: <a href=\"/wiki/Range_ambiguity_resolution\" title=\"Range ambiguity resolution\">range ambiguity resolution</a></div>\n<p>The <a href=\"/wiki/Range_ambiguity_resolution\" title=\"Range ambiguity resolution\">range ambiguity resolution</a> techniques used with <a href=\"/wiki/Medium_pulse_repetition_frequency\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"Medium pulse repetition frequency\">medium pulse repetition frequency</a> radar can be seen as a special case of the Chinese remainder theorem.\n</p>\n<h3><span id=\"Dedekind.27s_theorem\"></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Dedekind's_theorem\">Dedekind's theorem</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/w/index.php?title=Chinese_remainder_theorem&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26\" title=\"Edit section: Dedekind&#039;s theorem\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><b>Dedekind's theorem on the linear independence of characters.</b> Let <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">M</span> be a <a href=\"/wiki/Monoid\" title=\"Monoid\">monoid</a> and <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">k</span> an <a href=\"/wiki/Integral_domain\" title=\"Integral domain\">integral domain</a>, viewed as a monoid by considering the multiplication on <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">k</span>. Then any finite family <span class=\"texhtml\">(&#160;<i>f<sub>i</sub></i>&#160;)<sub><i>i</i>\u2208<i>I</i></sub></span> of distinct monoid homomorphisms <span class=\"texhtml\">&#160;<i>f<sub>i</sub></i>&#160;: <i>M</i> \u2192 <i>k</i></span> is linearly independent. In other words, every family <span class=\"texhtml\">(<i>\u03b1<sub>i</sub></i>)<sub><i>i</i>\u2208<i>I</i></sub></span> of elements <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>\u03b1<sub>i</sub></i> \u2208 <i>k</i></span> satisfying \n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}f_{i}=0}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <munder>\n          <mo>&#x2211;<!-- \u2211 --></mo>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n            <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n            <mi>I</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </munder>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>&#x03B1;<!-- \u03b1 --></mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>f</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>0</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}f_{i}=0}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3c1edf2d8866c4ea8fecfe32935633639b66cd72\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:12.229ex; height:5.676ex;\" alt=\"\\sum_{i \\in I}\\alpha_i f_i = 0\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>must be equal to the family <span class=\"texhtml\">(0)<sub><i>i</i>\u2208<i>I</i></sub></span>.\n</p><p><b>Proof.</b> First assume that <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">k</span> is a field, otherwise, replace the integral domain <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">k</span> by its quotient field, and nothing will change. We can linearly extend the monoid homomorphisms <span class=\"texhtml\">&#160;<i>f<sub>i</sub></i>&#160;: <i>M</i> \u2192 <i>k</i></span> to <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">k</span>-algebra homomorphisms <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>F<sub>i</sub></i>&#160;: <i>k</i>[<i>M</i>] \u2192 <i>k</i></span>, where <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>k</i>[<i>M</i>]</span> is the <a href=\"/wiki/Monoid_ring\" title=\"Monoid ring\">monoid ring</a> of <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">M</span> over <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">k</span>. Then, by linearity, the condition\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}f_{i}=0,}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <munder>\n          <mo>&#x2211;<!-- \u2211 --></mo>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n            <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n            <mi>I</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </munder>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>&#x03B1;<!-- \u03b1 --></mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>f</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>0</mn>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}f_{i}=0,}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/409b413bbc8afd6feb999cc8fb18911424495c29\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:12.876ex; height:5.676ex;\" alt=\"\\sum_{i\\in I}\\alpha_i f_i = 0,\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>yields\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}F_{i}=0.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <munder>\n          <mo>&#x2211;<!-- \u2211 --></mo>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n            <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n            <mi>I</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </munder>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>&#x03B1;<!-- \u03b1 --></mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>F</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>0.</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}F_{i}=0.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d947c812b95c827cf3b41b90d61df5def3edc3ec\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:13.231ex; height:5.676ex;\" alt=\"\\sum_{i \\in I}\\alpha_i F_i = 0.\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Next, for <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>i</i>, <i>j</i> \u2208 <i>I</i>; <i>i</i> \u2260 <i>j</i></span> the two <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">k</span>-linear maps <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>F<sub>i</sub></i>&#160;: <i>k</i>[<i>M</i>] \u2192 <i>k</i></span> and <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>F<sub>j</sub></i>&#160;: <i>k</i>[<i>M</i>] \u2192 <i>k</i></span> are not proportional to each other. Otherwise <span class=\"texhtml\">&#160;<i>f<sub>i</sub></i>&#160;</span> and <span class=\"texhtml\">&#160;<i>f<sub>j</sub></i>&#160;</span> would also be proportional, and thus equal since as monoid homomorphisms they satisfy: <span class=\"texhtml\">&#160;<i>f<sub>i</sub></i>&#160;(1) = 1 = &#160;<i>f<sub>j</sub></i>&#160;(1)</span>, which contradicts the assumption that they are distinct.\n</p><p>Therefore, the kernels <span class=\"texhtml\">Ker <i>F<sub>i</sub></i></span> and <span class=\"texhtml\">Ker <i>F<sub>j</sub></i></span> are distinct. Since <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>k</i>[<i>M</i>]/Ker <i>F<sub>i</sub></i> \u2245 <i>F<sub>i</sub></i>(<i>k</i>[<i>M</i>]) = <i>k</i></span> is a field, <span class=\"texhtml\">Ker <i>F<sub>i</sub></i></span> is a maximal ideal of <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>k</i>[<i>M</i>]</span> for every <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>i</i> \u2208 <i>I</i></span>. Because they are distinct and maximal the ideals <span class=\"texhtml\">Ker <i>F<sub>i</sub></i></span> and <span class=\"texhtml\">Ker <i>F<sub>j</sub></i></span> are coprime whenever <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>i</i> \u2260 <i>j</i></span>. The Chinese Remainder Theorem (for general rings) yields an isomorphism:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display:              <mo>&#x220F;<!-- \u220f --></mo>\n                  <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                    <mi>i</mi>\n                    <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n         <mtr>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi mathvariant=\"normal\">&#x03A6;<!-- \u03a6 --></mi>\n                <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n                <mi>x</mi>\n  <msub>\n                        <mi>F</mi>\n                        <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                          <mi>i</mi>\n                        </mrow>\n    </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\Phi :k[M]&amp;\\to \\prod _{i\\in I}k[M]/\\mathrm {Ker} F_{i}\\\\\\Phi (x)&amp;=\\left(x+\\mathrm {Ker} F_{i}\\right)_{i\\in I}\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bd5d28277427dfee1e915ad6e9aeae4655e41f44\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -3.838ex; width:28.44ex; height:8.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\begin{aligned}\\Phi :k[M]&amp;\\to \\prod _{{i\\in I}}k[M]/{\\mathrm  {Ker}}F_{i}\\\\\\Phi (x)&amp;=\\left(x+{\\mathrm  {Ker}}F_{i}\\right)_{{i\\in I}}\\end{aligned}}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>is surjective. Under the isomorphisms <span class=\"texhtml\"><i>k</i>[<i>M</i>]/Ker <i>F<sub>i</sub></i> \u2192 <i>F<sub>i</sub></i>(<i>k</i>[<i>M</i>]) = <i>k</i>,</span> the map <span class=\"texhtml\">\u03a6</span> corresponds to:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\psi :k[M]&amp;\\to \\prod _{i\\in I}k\\\\\\psi (x)&amp;=\\left[F_{i}(x)\\right]_{i\\in I}\\end{aligned}}}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n          <mtable columnalign=\"right left right left right left right left right left right left\" rowspacing=\"3pt\" columnspacing=\"0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em\" displaystyle=\"true\">\n            <mtr>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi>&#x03C8;<!-- \u03c8 --></mi>\n                <mo>:</mo>\n                <mi>k</mi>\n                <mo stretchy=\"false\">[</mo>\n                <mi>M</mi>\n                <mo stretchy=\"false\">]</mo>\n              </mtd>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi></mi>\n                <mo stretchy=\"false\">&#x2192;<!-- \u2192 --></mo>\n                <munder>\n                  <mo>&#x220F;<!-- \u220f --></mo>\n                  <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                    <mi>i</mi>\n                    <mo>&#x2208;<!--      <mtd>\n                <mi>&#x03C8;<!-- \u03c8 --></mi>\n                <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n                <mi>x</mi>\n                <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n              </mtd>\n              <mtd>\n                <mi></mi>\n                <mo>=</mo>\n                <msub>\n                  <mrow>\n                    <mo>[</mo>\n                    <mrow>\n                      <msub>\n                        <mi>F</mi>\n                        <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                          <mi>i</mi>\n                        </mrow>\n                      </msub>\n                      <mo stretchy=\"false\">(</mo>\n                      <mi>x</mi>\n                      <mo stretchy=\"false\">)</mo>\n                    </mrow>\n                    <mo>]</mo>\n                  </mrow>\n                  <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                    <mi>i</mi>\n                    <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n                    <mi>I</mi>\n                  </mrow>\n                </msub>\n              </mtd>\n            </mtr>\n          </mtable>\n        </mrow>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\psi :k[M]&amp;\\to \\prod _{i\\in I}k\\\\\\psi (x)&amp;=\\left[F_{i}(x)\\right]_{i\\in I}\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c9598795d3005ba9a366342806215a44e9427b4c\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -3.838ex; width:21.699ex; height:8.843ex;\" alt=\"{\\begin{aligned}\\psi :k[M]&amp;\\to \\prod _{{i\\in I}}k\\\\\\psi (x)&amp;=\\left[F_{i}(x)\\right]_{{i\\in I}}\\end{aligned}}\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Now,\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}F_{i}=0}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <munder>\n          <mo>&#x2211;<!-- \u2211 --></mo>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n            <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n            <mi>I</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </munder>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>&#x03B1;<!-- \u03b1 --></mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>F</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>0</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}F_{i}=0}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4369dfbdabe8cf4df3b460a51d2abbafca558e98\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:12.585ex; height:5.676ex;\" alt=\"\\sum_{i \\in I}\\alpha_i F_i = 0\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>yields\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}u_{i}=0}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <munder>\n          <mo>&#x2211;<!-- \u2211 --></mo>\n          <mrow <mi>&#x03B1;<!-- \u03b1 --></mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>u</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"texhtml\">(<i>u<sub>i</sub></i>)<sub><i>i</i>\u2208<i>I</i></sub></span> in the image of the map <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">\u03c8</span>. Since <span class=\"texhtml mvar\" style=\"font-style:italic;\">\u03c8</span> is surjective, this means that\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}u_{i}=0}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <munder>\n          <mo>&#x2211;<!-- \u2211 --></mo>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n            <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n            <mi>I</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </munder>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>&#x03B1;<!-- \u03b1 --></mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>u</mi>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>0</mn>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\sum _{i\\in I}\\alpha _{i}u_{i}=0}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/73cc1a7b14a45c49148665a9dfc122ccf481d768\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:12.42ex; height:5.676ex;\" alt=\"\\sum_{i \\in I}\\alpha_i u_i = 0\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>for every vector\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class=\"mwe-math-element\"><span class=\"mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y\" style=\"display: none;\"><math xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML\"  alttext=\"{\\displaystyle \\left(u_{i}\\right)_{i\\in I}\\in \\prod _{i\\in I}k.}\">\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n      <mstyle displaystyle=\"true\" scriptlevel=\"0\">\n        <msub>\n          <mrow>\n            <mo>(</mo>\n            <msub>\n              <mi>u</mi>\n              <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n                <mi>i</mi>\n              </mrow>\n            </msub>\n            <mo>)</mo>\n          </mrow>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n            <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n            <mi>I</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n        <munder>\n          <mo>&#x220F;<!-- \u220f --></mo>\n          <mrow class=\"MJX-TeXAtom-ORD\">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n            <mo>&#x2208;<!-- \u2208 --></mo>\n            <mi>I</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </munder>\n        <mi>k</mi>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding=\"application/x-tex\">{\\displaystyle \\left(u_{i}\\right)_{i\\in I}\\in \\prod _{i\\in I}k.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src=\"https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9e09cf5a30dc74601447b8b996260e6aa8b878fb\" class=\"mwe-math-fallback-image-inline\" aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:14.718ex; height:5.676ex;\" alt=\"\\left(u_i\\right)_{i \\in I} \\in \\prod_{i \\in I}k.\"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Consequently, <span class=\"texhtml\">(<i>\u03b1<sub>i</sub></i>)<sub><i>i</i>\u2208<i>I</i></sub> = (0)<sub><i>i</i>\u2208<i>I</i></sub></span>.
